French New Parliament Opens Under Tight Police Security; Women Demonstrate for Suffrage; Socialist Cabinet to Be Formed Imminently 28

(Paris) The new Parliament, dominated by the Radical Party, held its first meeting today. Hundreds of police officers were on guard around the Chamber of Deputies. No members of the Sarraut cabinet attended. The meeting began with a speech by the oldest member, Charles, who solemnly declared France's desire for peace. Then, eleven committee members were elected to study the legality of the parliamentary re-election tomorrow, and then elect a new speaker. Prime Minister Sarraut will submit his resignation on Thursday. President Lebrun will then order Socialist leader Blum to form a new cabinet. Blum plans to announce his political views on the 9th or 11th and then request a vote of confidence from the Chamber of Deputies. The most noteworthy thing at today's meeting was that the 72 Communist members of parliament entered the chamber as a group. (National Telegram)

(Paris) The first meeting of the 16th French Chamber of Deputies was held this afternoon. The situation was very calm. At present, the topics of discussion among the members in the Chamber of Deputies lounge are concentrated on two points: one is the formal nomination of former Prime Minister Herriot as a candidate for Speaker of the Chamber of Deputies, and the other is the declaration made by Herriot, advocating strengthening the friendship between the United States and France and ensuring the resolution of the war debt issue. The Chamber of Deputies is scheduled to meet tomorrow to review the legality of the election of the members of parliament. There are currently more than 40 members of parliament who are suspected of being illegally elected, and some have demanded that their seats be revoked. Under the insistence of the Communist Party, the three most important members whose seats they want to revoke are: the former Speaker of the Chamber of Deputies, Puisson (originally a Socialist member who has now left the party); the right-wing member, Chiappe, who served as the police chief when the riots broke out in Paris on February 6th and is currently the chairman of the Paris City Council; and Doriot, who was originally a Communist member but broke away from the Communist Party a few years ago due to his opposition to the Third International's interference in French internal affairs and formed his own independent Communist Party. Furthermore, the Communist Party also intends to obtain one of the six Deputy Speaker positions in the Chamber of Deputies and has decided to nominate the Communist member, Duclos, as a candidate. Once the election takes place, if the parties belonging to the left-wing Popular Front unanimously vote in favor, Duclos will definitely be elected. If so, when other members make excessive noise at future meetings, Duclos will come forward as Deputy Speaker to warn them. This can be said to be an innovation in the history of the French Parliament (in previous parliaments, Communist members made the most noise and were often warned by the Speaker and Deputy Speakers). (1st, Havas dispatch)

(Paris) When the new French Parliament officially opened today, a demonstration for women's suffrage took place. Before the opening, many women carried placards with slogans such as "Congratulations to the Government on its Success, but Do Not Forget Women" and gathered around the Chamber of Deputies. When Charles (age 76), the oldest member of parliament, finished his speech, many women in the gallery suddenly displayed placards on the walls with the words "French Women Must Have the Right to Vote." Extremely left-wing members of parliament cheered and supported this movement, but ushers rushed to the gallery and tore down the placards. (1st, Reuters)

(Paris) The Senate reconvened at 3:10 PM today. Speaker Jananet, Prime Minister Sarraut, Minister Without Portfolio Pengou, and Minister of Public Works Sudant were all present in the cabinet seats. The meeting began with the Speaker's opening remarks, expressing condolences for the late Senator and former Finance Minister Cheron. All members listened quietly. The Speaker then read out various reports. Many women's rights activists held a demonstration and distributed leaflets in the gallery, demanding the right to vote. At the same time, the Speaker continued to read the reports. The demonstrators left the meeting voluntarily without waiting for the adjournment. The Speaker then adjourned the meeting at 3:25 PM. (2nd, Geneva dispatch)

Speculations on Candidates for the New French Cabinet 29

(Paris) The cabinet will soon be officially formed. According to information obtained by our correspondent, the following are the candidates: Léon Blum, leader of the orthodox Socialist Party, will definitely accept the mandate to form the cabinet, but he is unwilling to take on a ministerial portfolio due to the onerous duties of the Prime Minister. In addition, there will be two new features in the organization of the new cabinet: The merger of the three departments of Navy, Army and Air Force into a Ministry of National Defense, which will be headed by the leader of the Radical Socialist Party, former Prime Minister Daladier, who will also serve as Deputy Prime Minister (originally Minister of Justice concurrently). Underneath, there will be three Deputy Ministers, responsible for Army, Navy and Air Force affairs respectively, to be held by Radical Socialist Party members Lucas, Camponissi, and Cote (former Minister of Aviation). The Ministry of Foreign Affairs will be renamed as the "Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Overseas Affairs", to be held by the current Minister of Justice and Deputy Prime Minister Delbos (Radical Socialist Party). Underneath, there will be two Secretaries, one to be held by Republican Socialist Union MP Veyrières, specializing in the affairs of French North African territories, and one to be held by Radical Socialist Party MP Tedeschi or Party MP Mochet, specializing in the affairs of overseas colonies. Other appointments include Socialist Party MP Olivet as Minister of Finance, Socialist Party MP Salengro as Minister of Interior, and Radical Socialist Party MP Cadeau (current Secretary-General of the State Council) as Secretary. Socialist Party MP Monnet will be Minister of Agriculture, with Ms. Le Carre as Secretary. Socialist Party member Simand will be Minister of Commerce, and Socialist Party member Dassot will be Minister of Merchant Marine. It is generally believed that the new cabinet will also set up three Ministers Without Portfolio, one for Socialist Party Secretary-General Fauré, one for the current Minister of Public Works and Radical Socialist Party Senator Sudant, and one for Republican Socialist Union Senator Pengou. Among them, Sudant has not fully accepted, and Pengou will continue to serve as the permanent representative to the League of Nations. Although this list may be subject to change in the future, the main outline of the pre-selected candidates for the new Prime Minister, Léon Blum, will be no more than this. (2nd, Havas dispatch)

Arabs Use Modern Tactics to Attempt to Disrupt Jerusalem's Water Supply

British Representative Presents Annual Report, Explains Situation in Palestine

Geneva: The League of Nations Mandates Commission met today and will study the British government's annual report on Palestine and the mandated territory of Transjordan. The report stated that the number of Jewish immigrants to both territories from January to May this year was lower than in the same period last year. Despite the current unrest and frequent riots, the British government is determined to fulfill its duties and will not back down. The strength of the local police force has recently been increased, and British authorities have taken various measures to curb the activities of rioters and strike leaders. This policy will continue to be implemented to quickly quell the disturbances. Once order and peace are restored, the British government will send a commission to investigate the causes of the incidents and study the demands of both the Arab and Jewish communities. Soviet Union Discovers Artifacts Thousands of Years Old 41

Evidence of Contact Between China and Kazakhstan

Moscow Correspondence: The research team of the Kazakhstan Research Association has discovered valuable artifacts, proving that Kazakhstan and ancient China had contact. They discovered stone statues of women, warriors, and lions in several pastures, carved from brown hard stone. These artifacts date back thousands of years, and their style indicates that they were created by ancient Chinese artists. The most interesting find is a bronze mirror, also an ancient Chinese artifact. The back of the mirror features bas-relief carvings of flowers, leaves, hair, Chinese ducks, and butterflies, as well as Chinese characters. Metallurgists have found that the mirror is extremely hard, almost impossible to damage with a knife or file, yet ancient Chinese artists were able to create intricate carvings on this hard alloy. (TASS, May 9th)

The "Queen Mary" Completes Maiden Voyage 42

Takes Four Days and Twelve Hours; New York Gives Enthusiastic Welcome; White Star Line Plans to Build Sister Ship

(New York) The White Star Line's new ship, the "Queen Mary," docked here at 4:03 PM today, completing its maiden voyage. The entire city of New York enthusiastically welcomed the ship's arrival. According to official reports, the voyage took four days, twelve hours, and twenty-four minutes. The docking process, which lasted twenty-five minutes, was uneventful. However, one tugboat collided with the side of the "Queen Mary," nearly capsizing. The ship passed the inspection station at 2:27 PM amidst cheers and the sound of thousands of ships' horns. As it approached the pier at 50th Street, built at a cost of $10 million, millions of onlookers on shore cheered enthusiastically. All the major buildings were flying the national flag, and twelve airplanes appeared intermittently in the thick smoke emitted from the "Queen Mary's" funnels. Another fifty ships of various types raced to its side. The tips received by the ship's stewards totaled $25,000. In light of the chaos that occurred when the French ship "Normandie" first arrived, customs officials sent 250 inspectors aboard. (Reuters, 1st)

(London) The Daily Mail recently reported that the government has decided to subsidize the Cunard White Star Line with £5 million to build a new ship, designed to be similar to the Queen Mary. (Havas, 2nd)

Railway Bureau and Customs Report Situation of Japanese and Korean Ruffians Smuggling 60

The Gold Mausoleum Customs Supervisor's Office has the Same Report 61

(Nanjing) The railway bureau and customs have reported in detail via telegram about the situation of Japanese and Korean ruffians smuggling goods and forcing transport on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. Details are as follows: The Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau reported that according to the report from the Transportation Department on May 27, two carriages of rayon from the East Station to Jinan on the 26th lacked customs permits and a request was made via telegram asking for instructions. On the morning of the 27th, more than 20 Japanese and Korean ruffians came and acted with extreme barbarity and were unreasonable. It was impossible to restrain them and they were determined to forcibly remove the goods. However, the customs inspector Ye Yuchun had not yet arrived in Jinan. The Japanese Consulate dispatched Nakanishi Takeo to the station to negotiate, signing a certificate and promising to take all responsibility, stating that if this was not done, they would simply allow them to cause trouble and the consulate would not be responsible. As a result, the goods were taken. Also, according to a telegram from Tianjin Main Station on May 28, on the 27th, 50 Japanese and Korean people brought 105 bundles of untaxed rayon and 30 pieces of cigarette paper and forcibly boarded Train No. 305. Also, according to a telegram from Jinan on May 28, on the 28th, more than 10 Japanese and Korean people carrying more than 130 pieces of rayon and cigarette paper unloaded them from the third-class passenger carriage of train No. 305 and forcibly ordered coolies to carry them out of the station, behaving rudely and not listening to orders. Also, according to a telegram from Xuzhou on May 28, on the night of the 27th, train No. 401 arrived at the station with carriages of sugar transported from the East Station to Shangqiu, two carriages from the Beining Railway weighing 20 tons, carriage numbers 1532 and 1466, all without customs documents. Postal Delivery of Litigation Documents to Be Implemented from July 1st 79

Nanyang The Ministry of Justice, regarding the matter of enforcing postal delivery of litigation documents, previously decided by the National Judicial Conference and ordered by the Executive Yuan to handle, consulted with the Ministry of Communications. It was also agreed that the delivery certificate would be printed by the court, while the notification and reason report would be printed by the post office. Women's Cosmetics Contain Lead 82

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Health believes that women's cosmetic face powder often contains lead, which is extremely harmful. Samples were collected from various provinces and cities, totaling 832 types. After more than a year of precise chemical testing, it was found that 40% contained lead, 13% contained zinc, 0.06% contained both zinc and lead, and 47.4% contained no metals. The Jiaxiang tender powder sent for testing by the Hebei Civil Affairs Department contained as much as 78% lead. The French Heguibeigan powder, which sells well worldwide, also contained 25.95% lead. The Ministry is also planning a new powder formulation, which has been satisfactorily tested. (Central News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Four Japanese Military Department Chartered Ships Transport Japanese Troops to Tianjin 95

Divided into Six Trains to Open Beiping-Tianjin-Yuyuqin, the Number of Troops Has Increased to More Than 5,000, After the Fifth Train Departed, It Was Suddenly Bombed Outside Tianjin East Station

Tianjin Correspondence, Japan's increase of troops in North China, one of its troops, in addition to the troops sent to the first three batches of troops totaling more than 800 people at the same time as the Gua Dai troops on May 14 and 15, on the 29th, from the Army Ministry Chartered Ships Character Products, Speedy, Komayama, and Minghai, carrying troops and artillery cavalry battalions, the number of cavalry, including cavalry and artillery, counted more than 300 cavalry, infantry and artillery and artillery and cavalry, a total of more than 1,500 people, at 9:30 a.m. on the same day, Komayama Maru first drove to Tanggu from outside Dagukou, and docked at the Japanese Dayuan Wharf, cutting off more than 300 cavalry, more than 300 horses, and more than 1,000 pieces of military supplies, and at 6:50 p.m., Minghai Maru entered the port, and also docked at the Japanese Dayuan Wharf, carrying more than 500 infantry and military clothing and other supplies, and at 7:30 p.m., Character Products Maru entered the port, docked at Station No. 1 Wharf, carrying more than 500 mechanized chemical warfare vehicles and artillery teams, and 4 large tanks, 3 small ones, 5 armored vehicles, 5 heavy-duty long-distance military vehicles, 2 pedal cars, 1 messenger boat, and various military supplies, at 8:40 p.m., Speedy Maru entered the port, also docked at Station No. 1 Wharf, carrying 17 mountain guns and field guns, more than 100 light and heavy machine guns, more than 500 infantry, and a large number of military supplies and ammunition, after the ships docked at the wharf, the Japanese military headquarters immediately sent staff officer Ikeda, adjutant Otake, and many attached personnel to take care of it. After the Japanese troops landed, from 1:25 p.m. on the same day and 2:05 p.m., they took two special trains on the Beining Railway and went to Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao. The first train carried 150 infantry and 60 cavalry, the second train carried 300 infantry and artillery, hundreds of pieces of baggage, and 8 cannons. Both trains arrived at their destinations at 10:00 p.m. and 11:00 p.m. respectively. The third special train left Tanggu at 5:30 p.m., carrying more than 240 cavalry, 240 horses, 8 cannons, and more than 500 pieces of military supplies. It arrived in Tianjin at 6:30 p.m. and stopped at the East Station. The commander of the Japanese army, Tashiro, led senior staff officer Tadayasu Taro, senior adjutant Kawata Tsui Taro, and the staff of the headquarters to welcome them at the station. Consul Kishii, President of the Residents' Association Morikawa Teruta, the International Women's Association, the Veterans' Association, and Japanese elementary school students, totaling more than 1,000 people, also went to the station to wave flags to welcome them. The newly arrived Japanese army, commanded by Captain Noguchi, except for 140 people who got off the train and entered the Hekogji Japanese army camp, the rest returned to the original train and went to Fengtai at 7:15 p.m. The fourth special train left Tanggu at 7:10 p.m., carrying 520 infantry and 14 horses. It arrived at Tianjin Station at 8:20 p.m. The Japanese commander Tashiro still led his staff and overseas Chinese to welcome them. Among the troops, there were 320 people, led by Fukuda, who got off the train and marched into the newly built Japanese barracks in Li Mingzhuang, Dongjuzi, and the remaining 150 people left on the original train at 8:30 p.m. and went to Beiping and then to Tongzhou. The fifth special train was originally scheduled to arrive at 11:30 p.m. on the 29th, but because of the railway explosion between Tanggu and Tianjin, it was blocked at the dam and postponed to the 30th. It was changed to two trains and arrived in Tianjin at 5:50 a.m., carrying 550 infantry, 12 cannons, and countless military supplies. When it arrived at Tianjin East Station, 350 people got off the train and went to the Li Mingzhuang barracks, and 200 people left on the original train at 6:20 a.m. and went to Beiping. The sixth train arrived in Tianjin at 9:50 a.m. on the 30th, carrying a lot of military supplies, seven tanks of various sizes, five armored vehicles, three heavy-duty vehicles, and 4,000 gas masks, escorted by 50 infantrymen. When they arrived in Tianjin, they stopped at the station and were transported to the Hekogji and Dongjuzi Japanese army camps. According to the investigation, the new army sent from April 13, May 14, 15, 29, and 30, in addition to those staying in Tianjin, together with the teams landed from Qindao Yuguan, Tanggu, totaling more than 5,000 people, of which more than 1,800 people belonged to the troop rotation team, and the rest were so-called strengthening teams, which was still far from the number of a division stipulated by the Japanese military department. It was originally planned to arrive successively after June 5, but recently, because of the attention of Europe and the United States, and because of the proposal of our central government, although the Japanese side did not pay attention, it also did not want the world to know its military actions, so it declared to the outside world that the transportation of the new army had ended on the 29th, and would not come again in the future, but it was slightly heard that after the air eased slightly, it would use other methods to transport them continuously, so before mid-July, the Japanese troops stationed in North China would reach about 12,000, once the Guantai new barracks were completed, or it would be the time to complete this matter. On the night of the 29th, the fifth train of Japanese troops was originally scheduled to depart from Tanggu at 10:30 p.m. and arrive in Tianjin at 11:30 p.m. At 10:00 p.m., the Japanese military department sent a captain of the infantry, leading 38 armed soldiers, to the East Station to ask the Beining Road stationmaster to borrow a ballast car, open it to Xinhe, check the tracks, and meet the fifth train of soldiers. The stationmaster asked the transportation department for instructions, which said that the ballast car was dedicated to railway workers and could not be easily lent, and allowed only a special train to be attached. The Japanese army agreed, and the road party temporarily compiled and attached an engine and a first, second, and third class passenger car. At 10:10 p.m., it departed from the East Station. When it was about to leave the station, 20 Japanese civilians came and went with the car. The train was commanded by the Japanese captain all the way, stopping and stopping from time to time. The Japanese army and civilians also went up and down from time to time, seeming to check the track. Usually, a passenger train from Tianjin East Station to Zhang Guizhuang only takes ten minutes, but on this night, it took forty minutes to arrive. After entering the station, the Japanese captain instructed to stop moving forward immediately, saying that there was no need to go to Xinhe again, and wait until 4 a.m. on the 30th to return to Tianjin. Then the Japanese army and the Japanese civilians were divided into several groups, measuring the bridges and tracks with tape measures. After that, they gradually went farther and farther, and returned to Tianjin on foot until about 2 a.m. on the 30th. At 11:35 p.m., while the Japanese army was surveying near Zhang Guizhuang, suddenly a railway track one kilometer away from Tianjin East Station was suddenly blown up, two sleepers were broken, the rails were bent, and the track was blown into two deep pits. Zhang Guizhuang Station inspectors heard the sound and rushed to inspect it. Seeing that the track was destroyed, they rushed to Tianjin Station to report it. At that time, the first train to Pingjing had already departed from the East Station and was warned and stopped by the inspectors who rushed. The train then returned to Tianjin. The railway bureau also informed the Japanese military headquarters after receiving the report. The headquarters then sent staff officer Hayashi to accompany the staff of the transportation department of the railway bureau to the site for investigation and investigation of responsibility. The staff officer took a video on the spot and took it back to report. After the explosion on the railway track, the East Station was guarded by the Japanese military department with the assistance of the military police, monitoring the actions of the road staff and not allowing passengers to get on and off. It was not until after 3 a.m. on the 30th that the Japanese military department allowed the workers to go to the bombed area for repairs after negotiations with the railway bureau. The Japanese military headquarters then sent several armed soldiers to patrol near Zhang Guizhuang, not allowing pedestrians to pass and searching for suspects. At 4:50 a.m., traffic was restored, and the Japanese army's vigilance was slightly relaxed. The departure of the Pingjing train was delayed for five hours. At 5:10 a.m. on the 30th, it departed from Tianjin East. The Beining Railway Bureau immediately reported the matter to Pingfang after the incident. Sun Jidong, the director of the Tianjin Public Security Bureau, was also invited to talk by Fujii, the commander of the Japanese military police, on the night of the 29th, saying that when the fourth train of Japanese soldiers arrived in Tianjin, communist leaflets opposing the arrival of the Japanese army were found at the East Station at 8:20 p.m. on the 29th, and the Chinese side was aware of it in advance. Sun said he did not know, and Fujii asked Sun to pay attention. Sun returned to the bureau and immediately summoned the director of the third special district public security bureau to inquire and order an investigation into whether the Communist Party was distributing leaflets at the station. According to the investigation report, there was no such thing. When the railway track was destroyed, the Japanese side pointed out that it was done by undisciplined elements. At 9:00 a.m. on the 30th, Sugai, a captain of the Japanese military police, came to the Tianjin County Public Security Bureau to visit Bai Lunbi, the chief of the public security section, on the order of Tashiro, and inquired about the matter, believing that the area belonged to Tianjin County, and the bureau should be responsible. He went to visit Liu Jia, the Tianjin Security Commander, for instructions in the afternoon. Liu asked the Beining Road, the Municipal Government, and the Tianjin Public Security Bureau, but none of them had received any expressions from the Japanese side. In addition to the Municipal Public Security Bureau feeling that the responsibility for the area did not belong exclusively to the county bureau, it had ordered the third public security bureau to arrest the intruders within three days. On the one hand, the Security Command was assisting various agencies in investigating the truth and arresting the criminals, and on the other hand, it was carefully defending to avoid further incidents. Because of this incident, rumors spread in Tianjin, people were panicked, and there was a sense of unease. (May 30)

Song Zheyuan Convenes Cadre Meeting 96

Stabilizing the Local Area and Coping with the Current Situation. The Main Purpose Is to Maintain Sovereignty

Beiping Correspondence, the situation in Hebei and Chahar, since the Hebei-East problem has been unresolved for a long time, the diplomatic situation has gradually entered a state of silence, but in the recent half month, Japan has greatly increased its troops in North China, which has attracted the attention of all parties and the panic of Pingjin. Tianjin students marched on May 28, and students in Ping city also held gatherings, while ignorant people took the opportunity to spread rumors in Tianjin, causing people to become restless. Song Zheyuan, the chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Committee, in order to stabilize the local area and cope with the current situation, specially convened cadres of the 29th Army at the private residence in Wuyiku Hutong on the evening of the 30th to discuss everything until late at night before dispersing. More than ten people, including Qin Dechun, Zhang Zizhong, Xiao Zhenying, Feng Zhian, Liu Ruming, and Zhang Yueting, attended. In addition to making decisions on maintaining public order, they also discussed in detail the attitude they should take, and unanimously decided to safeguard national sovereignty. During the meeting, Xiao Zhenying's intention to resign as Tianjin mayor was unanimously retained, and Song ordered Xiao to return to Tianjin on the same day to dispel rumors. After receiving the order, Xiao went to Tianjin by car with Zhang Zizhong, chairman of Chahar, and Ren Yuandao, a member of the Foreign Affairs Committee, at 8 p.m. on the 31st, and Xiao will return to Ping again in two or three days.

Song Zheyuan's Talk

Song Zheyuan met with the press at 6 p.m. on the 30th, with a calm attitude, and talked in detail about the current situation. Here is a brief note on the left, "The Hebei-Chahar area has recently been plagued by rumors and unrest due to the increase of Japanese troops, which are all not credible. There has been no progress in the diplomatic situation. On the 28th and 29th, Matsumuro had two decisions to meet with me. The first day's discussion was about the international situation after the European War, and the second day's discussion was only Matsumuro's statement that he was responsible for the diplomatic negotiations, and nothing else was mentioned. On the 30th, I was supposed to meet again, but the meeting was canceled because Matsumuro did not visit. A Japanese newspaper in Tianjin on the 30th published a news item "Warning Song Zheyuan", and I intend to question him about it immediately. The point of contention in the Hebei-Chahar incident is the issue of sovereignty. All incidents can be discussed under the principle of equality and mutual benefit, and I have also explained to the other party that Chinese sovereignty must be respected. For example, the Japanese embassy police arrested two young men in the old Ministry of Punishments Street in Xidan the other day, which is an infringement of our national sovereignty. After negotiations, the two men have been released. As for the crackdown on the trafficking of drugs by Japanese and Korean vagrants, it has been resolved. All vagrants in the counties have been expelled from the country. As for Japan's increase of troops in North China and the establishment of the brigade headquarters stationed in Ping, the procedures are not in compliance, and I also intend to ask the Japanese side for an explanation. Now our main purpose is to maintain sovereignty. At this critical moment, I sincerely hope that the government will have a solution soon. The student parade does not harm public order, nor does it endanger the lives and property of foreigners, so foreigners have no reason to interfere."

Huainan Railway to Hold Opening Ceremony on June 5th; Simultaneously Commemorating the Sixth Anniversary of the Coal Mine 97

Wuhu Correspondence: The Huainan Coal Mine, under the jurisdiction of the National Government's Construction Committee, has seen a significant increase in production and a thriving business in recent years. The Huainan Railway, built for transporting coal, has also been in operation for half a year. The bituminous coal produced by the mine can now be transported daily by rail to Yuxi for storage. Moreover, over 10,000 tons have been transported from the Datong Mine near Kunlian in the past month. As a result, the Yuxi wharf is piled high with coal, and iron ships arrive in a continuous stream for loading. The once desolate Yuxi has now become a prosperous port. With the convenience of transportation provided by the Huainan Coal Mine Bureau, they are determined to develop the coal seams as much as possible. Current daily output exceeds 2,000 tons, and plans are in place to increase it to 4,000 to 5,000 tons, ensuring that the provinces of Central and Southern China will not suffer from a shortage of coal. The mine bureau has decided to combine two ceremonies – the completion of the railway and the sixth anniversary of the coal mine's opening – to be held on June 5th at the Jiulonggang Mine Bureau in Huaiyuan County. Invitees include officials from relevant organizations in Beijing, Shanghai, Ping, Tianjin, Wuhu, Hankou, Bengbu, major companies, the press, and representatives from various chambers of commerce, totaling over 500 people. Most of them will gather in Wuhu on the 3rd and depart from Yuxi by train on the morning of the 4th to attend the ceremony at the mine. The director of the mine bureau, Cheng Shifan, has already arrived in Yuxi from the bureau by train to prepare for the reception. The local products to be collected and sent along the route number in the hundreds. Their gathering together during the event will undoubtedly add much color to the commemorative meeting. The mine's history, production, railway construction process, and local products along the route are investigated separately as follows:

Coal Mine Development: Mining Area and Location

After the establishment of the National Government Construction Committee, given that Southern China relied on Northern mines for fuel, and since the Central Government established its capital in Nanjing, the Yangtze River basin has seen flourishing industry and commerce, with a concentration of population and an increasing demand for coal. However, most mines in North China were operated with foreign capital, and domestic coal production was limited. In order to promote domestic coal production and supply fuel to the Yangtze River region, the National Government began to research and plan a state-owned coal mine. In the 18th year [of the Republic], the Huainan mining area was surveyed and the Huainan Coal Mine Bureau was established. The mine is located on the south bank of the Huai River in northern Anhui Province, at the intersection of Huaiyuan, Fengtai, and Shou counties, with five mining areas: Jiulonggang, Dongshan, Changshan, Shangyao, and Xinchengkou. The five areas have a total area of over 22 square kilometers, with coal seam outcrops extending for 35 kilometers. Currently, mining is conducted in the Jiulonggang area, which is 52 kilometers in a straight line from Bengbu, 10 kilometers from the Luoyangzhen on the near bank of the Huai River, 10 kilometers by water from Huaiyuan, 35 kilometers from Shou County, and 200 kilometers in a straight line from the Yangtze River. The Dongshan area is six kilometers west of the Jiulonggang area. Drilling in that area has been completed, and well-sinking has commenced. The Datong Coal Mine lies between the Jiulonggang and Dongshan areas. The remaining three areas are all located north of the Jiulonggang area, approximately 12 kilometers away, arranged from southeast to northwest, extending for 17 kilometers.

Transportation and Coal Volume

A narrow-gauge railway, 12 kilometers long, has been built from the Jiulonggang area to Luohe. Coal is transported via this route to Luohezhen, and then by waterway via the Huai River to Bengbu, and from there by the Jinpu Railway to Pukou, for transfer to various ports along the Yangtze River (the freight is over four yuan per ton; with the completion of the Huainan Railway, it will only be two yuan, a reduction of more than one-half). However, when the water level of the Huai River is low in winter, only small boats of 20 to 30 tons can navigate, and there are various restrictions on vehicles and freight rates on the Jinpu Railway. With high costs, monthly shipments are less than 20,000 tons. Therefore, the mine cannot be developed without opening a railway to the Yangtze River. Thus, the idea of building a railway to the Yangtze River was present from the very beginning. However, due to the enormous costs and difficulty in raising funds, work was delayed until the spring of the 23rd year [of the Republic]. Construction was divided into four sections, and the line was opened to Chaoxian in September of the 24th year and fully opened in January of the 25th year. One can travel from the mine to the riverside from morning until evening, and all the transportation difficulties of the past can be eliminated. Regarding the reserves of the Huainan coalfield, opinions vary. A survey conducted by the Academia Sinica in the 21st year [of the Republic] found that the Jiulonggang mining area is 4,600 meters long. Assuming a mining depth of 1,000 meters and a specific gravity of 1.3 for the coal, the reserves are estimated at 71,700,000 tons. The Dongshan area is 2,800 meters long, with reserves of 43,700,000 tons, totaling 115,400,000 tons. Currently, the rock tunnel only penetrates 200 meters of the coal system, and there is the possibility of discovering new coal seams in the future. If we assume that half of the currently identified coal volume can be discovered in the future, then the two areas will have a total of 170,000,000 tons of coal. If we take 60% of this figure as the recoverable amount, there would still be 101,000,000 tons. If we consider half of that amount, the mine would have at least 50 million tons of coal available for extraction. The coal produced is high-volatile bituminous coal. According to tests conducted by the Fuel Research Laboratory of the Geological Survey, it is a low-carbon bituminous coal, suitable for burning in boilers and for producing coal gas. When mixed with medium-carbon bituminous coal, it can produce good metallurgical coke. Huainan coal is also suitable for low-temperature coking. According to research by the laboratory, each ton can yield more than 30 gallons of coal tar, a rare achievement among bituminous coals in the country. Currently, there are two well-sinking sites in the Jiulonggang mining area, one in the east plant and one in the west plant. The two plants are 16 kilometers apart. The coal currently sold is produced by both the east and west plants.

Songjiang: June 3rd Anti-Smoking Day Parade 98

For the June 3rd Anti-Smoking Day, the county government convened a meeting of various agencies and decided that at 8:00 AM on that day, all civil servants from various agencies would gather at the commissioner's office to form a parade and march through the streets. The confiscated smoking paraphernalia from closed cases was put on display at the First District Office from the day before, for public viewing. On the afternoon of the 3rd, the paraphernalia was burned at the small drill field. The anti-smoking speech competition for primary and secondary school students was held on the 1st and 2nd at the People's Education Hall, Yue Temple, and People's Library respectively, with a large audience. Prizes were awarded in the afternoon, with the prizes being donated by various agencies.

Suggestions for Widening Streets 99

Since the introduction of rickshaws to the city, the streets have become quite narrow. The county government discussed this issue at a policy meeting, agreeing that Zhongshan Street is the most prosperous area of the city, and that Changqiao Street and Fayuan South Street are important thoroughfares for automobile traffic, and all need to be widened. It was stipulated that the road surface be widened to seven meters, and the plan of "straightening by cutting off bends" was not adopted to avoid excessive losses. The existing shape of the road will be maintained, and half of the houses on both the upper and lower banks will be demolished. If there are no houses to be demolished on the lower bank, then the upper bank will be demolished. However, the government will form an evaluation committee, and the residents on the lower bank will compensate the land price to make up for the losses on the upper bank. After the resolution was passed, it was submitted to the provincial authorities for approval and implementation.

Suzhou: All Cocoon Markets Open for Business 100

Silkworm raising in various villages in Wuxian County has finished. Cocoon markets in places like Guangfu, Mudu, Shanrenqiao, Hengjing, and Dongshan have all opened for business and are purchasing fresh cocoons. The latest to open is in the West Dongting Mountain, scheduled to open on the 3rd to purchase cocoons. The Wuxian Silkworm Improvement Farm is concerned that private white cocoon smugglers may obstruct operations, so they dispatched a large number of inspectors to various villages on the 2nd to investigate. The price of cocoons is uniformly based on the resolution of the Wuxian Cocoon Industry Association, with improved varieties priced at 30 yuan as the standard and local varieties at 20 yuan. According to people in the cocoon industry, this year's cocoon production is very good, with an average yield of about 90%. However, because the price of mulberry leaves soared a week ago, silkworm farmers suffered heavy losses, so even though the harvest is good, they are still complaining.

At around 7:00 PM last night (the 30th), five bandits, each carrying a box gun, suddenly broke into the Qingji Company on Main Street. Two Years of Jiangsu's Anti-Smoking Efforts "Part 1" 105

— Yu Jingtang

Introduction

In the spring of the 23rd year [of the Republic], the Jiangsu Provincial Government formulated the Outline of the Jiangsu Province Limited-Term Anti-Smoking Measures, stipulating that general smokers must quit within four years in stages, while civil servants addicted to smoking were ordered to quit within one month. In the summer of the same year, the Provincial Government meeting passed the Organizational Regulations of the Jiangsu Province Anti-Smoking Committee, establishing eleven members, with a secretary underneath, divided into four sections: General Affairs, Investigation and Arrest, Licensing, and Auditing. Each section was headed by a section chief to preside over the anti-smoking affairs of the province. Each county also established a County Anti-Smoking Committee, with the county magistrate as the chairman, and also appointed a secretary, divided into four sections: General Affairs, Investigation and Arrest, Licensing, and Auditing. Each section had a chief. This is the general organizational structure of the provincial and county anti-smoking committees. The anti-smoking policy was implemented under the provincial and county anti-smoking committees for one year and three months. In August of the 24th year, in accordance with the instructions of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, anti-smoking affairs were divided into two departments: supervision and execution. The supervisory body was the provincial and county anti-smoking committees. The provincial execution matters were handled by the fifth section added to the Department of Civil Affairs, and the county execution matters were handled by the anti-smoking section added to the county government. All anti-smoking laws and regulations remained the same, striving to be effective in order to achieve the goal of complete prohibition as scheduled. Almost another ten months have passed. Now, on the occasion of the second anniversary of the "June 3rd" Anti-Smoking Day in the 25th year, the past processing of the matters are summarized as follows:

1. Registration of Smokers

The province has conducted a total of three registration efforts. The first effort was a general registration, which took place in the summer and autumn of the 23rd year, lasting four months, registering a total of 184,980 smokers. In the winter of the same year, a supplementary registration was conducted for one month, registering 12,708 smokers. This spring, another self-renewal registration of smokers was conducted, lasting one and a half months, registering 105,858 smokers. The above three registrations totaled 303,546 smokers. Among them, 17,445 people were unable to obtain licenses and were sent to the addiction treatment center for free detoxification. There were 6,920 people who died or moved and could not be ordered to obtain licenses. The actual number of licensed individuals was 279,181, of which 27,264 held Class A licenses and 251,917 held Class B licenses.

2. Establishment of Addiction Treatment Hospitals and Centers

When the province began implementing the anti-smoking policy in the 23rd year, it planned to establish addiction treatment hospitals and centers in each county. In October of the same year, a provincial addiction treatment hospital was established in the provincial capital, also handling addiction treatment affairs in Zhenjiang, with an initial operating cost of 3,500 yuan and monthly operating expenses of 2,000 yuan. At the same time, in order to research the standards and methods of addiction treatment and investigation, a research department was attached to the provincial hospital, hiring experts to specialize in the matter. The other sixty counties also established addiction treatment centers one after another in November of the 23rd year, with an average initial operating cost of 1,500 yuan per center and average monthly operating expenses of 500 yuan per center. Subsequently, because each county's addiction treatment center admitted, treated, forcibly treated, and investigated drug offenders, with an average of more than 150 people per month, the original number of beds, instruments, medicines, and other facilities related to treatment, investigation, and entertainment were insufficient. After investigation, expansion was granted according to the actual local conditions. It is now estimated that the capacity of addiction treatment hospitals and centers in the province can accommodate 5,327 smokers at the same time. Considering that there are two batches per month, it can accommodate 10,654 people. Moreover, since the local finances of each county in the province are strained and county hospitals have not been generally established, and those that have been established still lack content and equipment, in order to promote local medical and health care universally, it was ordered that all those with previously established county hospitals whose equipment was already relatively complete should uniformly establish internal and surgical clinics within the addiction treatment centers. The required initial and operating expenses are to be allocated from the addiction treatment income. It is now estimated that a total of 17 counties, including Danyang and Yangzhong, have been established, and 30 counties, including Binying, are actively preparing to do so.

3. Forced Addiction Treatment for Smokers

The province has a large number of licensed smokers, and it is difficult for addiction treatment hospitals and centers to admit and treat them all at once. Therefore, based on the Outline of the Limited-Term Anti-Smoking Measures, an addiction treatment year was stipulated and a planned, batch-by-batch forced addiction treatment was implemented. It began on October 1st of the 23rd year, in stages of four years, with a requirement to treat at least one-quarter of the total number of registered smokers each year. As for the order of priority of the batch-by-batch treatment, it was stipulated that those under the age of 30 should be treated later, in the first year; those between 31 and 40 years of age should be treated in the second year; those between 41 and 50 years of age should be treated in the third year; and those over 51 years of age should be treated in the fourth year. If the target of one-quarter is not reached in one year, the smokers who should be treated in the next year should be treated in advance to make up the quarter. The standards for the order of priority and advance treatment of the smokers to be treated in the same year are as follows: 1. Those with younger ages are prioritized; 2. If the ages are the same, those with lighter smoking habits are prioritized; 3. If the ages and smoking habits are the same, the county decides. The list of smokers to be treated in each batch must be announced at least two weeks in advance and notified separately, and a copy must be reported to the province for record. Once a licensed smoker is notified for addiction treatment, their license will become invalid from the date of notification. Those who refuse to be treated after the deadline will be detained and forcibly treated. Smokers in the province have been undergoing forced addiction treatment since October of the 23rd year. Excluding those who died or moved and could not be treated, a total of 94,224 smokers have been treated as of April of this year. Moreover, 2,528 smokers were undergoing treatment in April.

4. Training and Relief for Smokers

According to the current anti-smoking situation in the province, it has been possible to unify and manage smokers and implement treatment within a limited time. However, those who voluntarily enter for treatment are sincere, and can they stop resuming smoking after being released? Smokers are generally weak and mostly poor and helpless. How to provide relief after treatment has become an important issue. Therefore, in the winter of the 23rd year, a training program for smokers was formulated. Last year, a savings program and smoker factories were also established to seek remedies. The training program is divided into knowledge training, individual talks, spiritual lectures, physical exercise, labor, reflection, self-government training, entertainment, and other items. Among them, knowledge training, individual talks, and spiritual lectures are given by members of the county anti-smoking committee, personnel from other agencies, and the director and doctors of the center. As for livelihood relief, the Jiangsu Farmers Bank has a savings incentive program for smokers, and the province has established smoker factories in districts. Since April of last year, one factory has been established in each district of Nantong, Tongshan, and Yancheng (the Yancheng factory is not yet fully established). These factories are larger in scale and require more funding, so they cannot be established universally at once. In addition, Wujin has established a smoker skills training workshop, and Zhenjiang has established a smoker rehabilitation center (to be continued).

Today's "June 3rd" Anti-Smoking Commemoration: All Sectors Hold a Meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce; National Anti-Drug Association Issues a Painful Declaration 106

Today is the 97th anniversary of "June 3rd," and the National Government has designated this day as Anti-Smoking Commemoration Day. The city party headquarters will hold a commemorative meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce at 10:00 AM today, gathering people from all sectors of the city. The presidium has nominated eleven institutions and organizations: the city party headquarters, the city government, the garrison command, the public security bureau, the reporting commissioner's office, the anti-smoking committee, the National Anti-Drug Association, the city farmers' association, the general labor union, the city education association, and the city chamber of commerce. After the commemorative meeting, a mass rally will be held at the Tianhou Palace open space to burn opium, drugs, and smoking paraphernalia. To expand publicity, celebrities from all walks of life have been specially invited to give speeches on the radio about anti-smoking and anti-drug efforts. Those invited include Mayor Wu, Wu Kaixian, Pan Gongzhan, Yang Hu, Wu Xingya, Ma Liang, Cai Jinjun, Li Tingan, Tong Hangbai, Jiang Huaishu, Cai Hongtian, Du Yuesheng, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, and others. At the same time, major daily newspapers throughout the city will publish special anti-smoking supplements, and all institutions, organizations, and schools throughout the city will celebrate by hanging flags. When performers present their art, they will intersperse anti-smoking propaganda to attract public attention.

The China National Anti-Drug Association, commemorating the 97th anniversary of Commissioner Lin Zexu's burning of opium at Humen today, in addition to coordinating with various institutions and organizations in the city to hold a grand commemoration at the City Chamber of Commerce, has also issued the Anti-Drug Monthly and the June 3rd Commemorative Special in advance, and notified anti-drug organizations across the country to step up the anti-drug movement and carry out large-scale publicity to awaken the public. The association's commemorative declaration is recorded below: "Today is the 97th anniversary of the burning of opium at Humen by the anti-smoking pioneer Lin Wenzhong Gong. We recall our predecessors and look at the difficulties of the time, feeling a sense of emotion. The decline of our national strength, the poverty of the people, the rampant foreign aggression, and the shrinking of our territory are all rooted in the scourge of opium. Lin Zexu saw this in those days and could not bear to see the spread of opium and the shaking of the national foundation. He stood alone against all opposition and vigorously advocated anti-smoking efforts, even daring to fight against the British. His spirit of safeguarding national rights and preserving national territory is the supreme glory of our nation and should be admired by all generations and admired by all nations. Looking back today, the decline of our national strength and the rampant foreign aggression are even worse than in the past. Those who are scheming to destroy our country and exterminate our nation are protecting vagrant scoundrels to spread drugs everywhere as a prelude to aggression. The facts are all there and cannot be denied. The large-scale opium production and public sale in the four northeastern provinces, the mass production of drugs, and the encouragement of smoking have long been seen by the world and need no further explanation. Recently, in counties in eastern Hebei and the cities of Beijing and Tianjin, Japanese and Korean vagrants have set up trading houses everywhere and openly sell drugs. They can be seen everywhere in the streets and alleys. Fuzhou and Xiamen, close to Taiwan, are even more unspeakable because of the rampant drug scourge. The concessions in Hankou are filled with drug factories, producing more than 10,000 catties each year. The corners of the Hongkou district in northern Shanghai are also studded with opium dens and drug shops, all of which destroy the livelihood of our people and cut through the bodies of our people. All of these have been investigated and revealed by the association. Recently, representatives from various countries have spoken out for justice at the League of Nations General Assembly, advocating for its eradication. It is clear that justice is on our side and cannot be concealed, which is gratifying. However, the flow of poison has spread so widely and penetrated so deeply into society. How can we stand idly by and ignore it? The government has now made a determined plan to ban smoking, and the international community is also showing good intentions to help, so the responsibility for clearing drugs lies with the efforts of our people. We must know that if the scourge of drugs is not eliminated for a single day, our country's smoking ban will never be able to achieve its goal. If the scourge of drugs is not eliminated for a single day, the Chinese nation will never have the hope of turning itself around. People are scheming to harm us. Seizing cities and land is not enough, and now they are using this deadly drug to destroy our country and exterminate our race. In order to survive, we should rise up and follow the example of Lin Gong, unite our forces, and fight this drug to the death. We also hope that government leaders will see themselves as Lin Gong, rise up to defend our territory, and clear away drugs, lest our beautiful land be lost to others and all 400 million people become opium addicts. Then today's commemoration will be in vain. This is our declaration."

Committee for Raising Funds to Purchase Aircraft as a Birthday Gift Holds First Tea Party Yesterday; Reports on the Purpose and Methods of Fundraising 107

The Shanghai Municipal Committee for Raising Funds to Present the Government with Aircraft in Commemoration of Chairman Chiang’s Fiftieth Birthday, initiated by the municipal government and its affiliated agencies, as well as various organizations, schools, and guilds, held its first tea party yesterday. Attendees included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau Xu Fu, Secretary Wang Zhinan of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Tong Xingbai of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhou Xuexiang of the Shanghai General Labor Union, Yu Zuoting of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Wang Xiaolai of the Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association, Gu Xinyi of the Food Grain Industry Guild, and representatives from the National Medical Association, the National Pharmaceutical Association, the Glass Industry Guild, the Liang Shaojiu (Liquor) Industry Guild, the Tu Huangjiu (Local Yellow Wine) Industry Guild, the Carpet Industry Guild, the Western Tobacco Industry Guild, the Universities Joint Association, the Performing Arts Joint Association, the Chinese Buddhist Association, the Shanghai Buddhist Association, the China Vocational Education Society, the Hebei Fellow-Villagers Association, the Hubei Fellow-Villagers Association, the Fujian Fellow-Villagers Association, the Guangdong Fellow-Villagers Association, the Central Bank, the Silk Industry Bank, the International Law and Trade Association, the Municipal Museum, the First Special District Local Court, and others, as well as Huang Jinrong, Zhao Jinqing, Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Shouyong, Zhang Xiaolin, and more than three hundred others.

Chairman's Speech

The meeting was held in the restaurant on the ninth floor of the YMCA. In the center were the flags of the Party and the nation and the emblem of the China Aviation Association, along with photos from past aircraft purchase and naming ceremonies. The hall was filled with Party and national flags, creating a magnificent and solemn atmosphere. The presidium consisted of Wang Xiaolai, Wu Tiecheng, Pan Gongzhan, Zhang Shouyong, and Yu Zuoting, with Chen Shuo as the recorder. After the meeting began, Wang Xiaolai delivered an opening speech, stating that all circles in Shanghai had initiated a fundraising campaign to purchase aircraft to celebrate Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday. He expressed gratitude for the presence of so many guests to discuss the progress. He said that various countries in the world that adhere to a single ideology, support a single leader, and work together wholeheartedly are invariably strong. Chairman Chiang is our national leader who toils for the country. All our people should support him wholeheartedly. Therefore, raising funds to purchase aircraft is a demonstration of public opinion. He hoped that everyone would work together under the leadership of Mayor Wu.

Mayor's Speech

Mayor Wu then delivered a speech, stating that since Shanghai initiated the movement to "Use Aviation to Save the Nation" two years ago, it had inspired a nationwide surge of enthusiasm. It not only awakened the national public's passion for saving the nation through aviation but also made the national public realize that building an air force is the fundamental and most crucial task of national defense construction today. Shanghai's first fundraising campaign two years ago achieved a result of over 1.3 million yuan, purchasing 18 aircraft and donating them to the government. Last year, the Aviation Association resolved to launch a second campaign. This year also marks Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday. Therefore, the association invited people from all walks of life to launch a fundraising campaign, simultaneously notifying the whole country to hold it together. Up to now, Shanghai has raised over 200,000 yuan, and counting reports from all over, the total is expected to reach 4 million yuan. Shanghai plans to raise 1 million yuan, purchase ten fighters, form them into a squadron, and present them to the government as a birthday memorial for Chairman Chiang. Today, we have invited leaders from all walks of life to participate in discussing fundraising methods so that we can achieve our goal as scheduled. Currently, there are over 280 organizations and 371 individuals who have joined the initiative, and more continue to join. This enthusiastic participation proves that the citizens have recognized the urgency of air force construction. With this enthusiastic atmosphere, 1 million yuan should not be difficult to raise. Our national crisis did not begin today, but it is becoming increasingly serious. Empty talk of saving the nation will only lead to fruitless labor. It is hoped that we will firmly believe in one ideology, namely the Three Principles of the People, and support the leader with one heart and one mind, putting our lives on the line. Only then will saving the nation have practical meaning and power, and the national crisis can be resolved.

Chairman's Report

Wang Xiaolai then reported that twelve fundraising methods had been established, and he hoped that everyone would express their opinions as much as possible. He now intended to report the pledges from various parties: the Food Grain Guild pledged to donate one aircraft, the Exchange Association pledged to donate one aircraft, Tao Guilin donated 1,000 yuan, the entire staff of the Municipal Public Security Bureau jointly donated 11,000 yuan, the Western Pharmaceutical Guild donated 1,000 yuan, the Municipal Bank Association donated 10,000 yuan, and the Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association is currently planning to raise 100,000 yuan. In the future, meetings will be convened every half month to report progress. As for the methods, ten levels such as Heaven, Earth, Central, and Righteous are stipulated. It is hoped that schools and organizations will raise funds on their own and contact the China Aviation Association and the Recruitment Team Leader's Office at any time. If there are slight discrepancies with the specified levels and numbers, it will not be a problem. It is only hoped that everyone will work hard to make pledges and achieve the goal as soon as possible.

Fundraising Announcement

The committee's fundraising announcement stated: "Respectfully addressing you, the fifteenth day of the ninth month of the summer Zheng Dinghai year (October 29th) is the fiftieth birthday of the current President of the Executive Yuan and Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek. The people of the whole country are dancing and singing in celebration. In ancient times, when celebrating someone's birthday, people composed poems and songs, transmitted praises, offered jade and silk to express their sincerity, or presented garments to convey their best wishes. Nowadays, these have become common practices. However, Mr. Chiang is dedicated to public service, values simplicity, and sets an example for his subordinates and the entire nation. If we were to follow the old customs, offering flattery and praise, it would not only violate the spirit of the new era but also greatly contradict the sincerity from the heart. Therefore, all flowery language is meaningless. Moreover, the national crisis today is urgent. Internally, the rebellious atmosphere has not been cleared, and externally, hidden worries lurk. Mr. Chiang, with his Shen Fu-like demeanor, bears the weight of the military and the nation. He toils faithfully for the country, from dawn till dusk. For ten years, our people have been able to live and work in peace, without being alarmed by violence. Tracing the source, all of this is a gift from Mr. Chiang. Now that his birthday is approaching, we respectfully follow the Yuan's order, instructing the whole country not to be extravagant. This further demonstrates his dedication to public service and selflessness. We should be even more motivated to repay him with our efforts. We, the colleagues, are deeply grateful for his kindness and recall his noble spirit. We believe that since Mr. Chiang has dedicated himself to the country, we should also seek ways to repay the country in order to repay Mr. Chiang. This is the best way to respond to his special concern and comply with public opinion. With the consensus of the public, we should take the lead in contributing. We have heard that when the German leader, Mr. Hitler, celebrated his birthday, the people of his country purchased aircraft to express their congratulations. This demonstrates love for the leader and also love for the country, and it has become a beautiful story spread throughout the world, praised as a grand event. How can our people lag behind? Purchasing aircraft to pay tribute is the unanimous opinion of the public. You, the leaders of all fields, are admired by the public. With your virtue of acting righteously, you have never been behind others. Please contribute your private funds to this great cause, which fulfills the meaning of repaying the country and expresses the sincerity of offering congratulations. We hope for your understanding and look forward to your clear instructions. We hereby make this special announcement. We wish you peace and tranquility.

Executive Yuan Partially Approves Measures to Prevent Smuggling and Import Tariff Rates 108

Executive Yuan Approval: The Electrical and Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association received Approval No. 570 from the Executive Yuan: "Submitted by Cai Shengbai, Chairman of the Shanghai Electrical and Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association, on May 12, 25th year, regarding rampant smuggling in North China, requesting prompt adoption of effective measures to stop it. The submission has been noted. Measures to prevent smuggling in North China have been planned and will be implemented soon. There will be no reduction in import tariff rates. Please be informed." This approval was also received from the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance: "Approval No. Guanzi 955: The submission has been noted. The Ministry is currently actively planning preventive measures for smuggling matters, in order to achieve results and protect industry and commerce. There is no reduction in the originally determined tariff rates. You should be informed."

Ministry Telegram: The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Local Association, and the Banking and Money Industry Associations, four groups, previously telegraphed the government regarding smuggling in North China, requesting measures to prevent it and supporting the position of not reducing tariffs. The associations received a reply telegram from the Ministry of Finance yesterday: "Your telegram has been read and noted. The Ministry is currently actively planning preventive measures for smuggling matters, in order to achieve results and protect industry and commerce. The Provisional Regulations for Punishing Tax Evasion and Smuggling issued by the Central Government have been distributed for information and announced for implementation. Please be informed." Electrical and Silk Weaving Industry: Methods to Prevent Smuggling; Industry Should Conduct Self-Inspection; Factory Fabrics Should Be Certified by the Association 109

The Shanghai Electrical and Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association held a special emergency joint meeting of directors and supervisors yesterday to prevent smuggling. Committee members Cai Shengbai, Wang Shiqiang, Tao Shaojiang, Jin Deqing, Gao Shiheng, Tong Xinbo, and Qian Boxi (Wang Shiqiang representing) attended. After Chairman Cai Shengbai reported on routine matters, Committee member Gao Shiheng proposed that, according to customs reports, the amount of rayon used by the silk weaving industry that is smuggled is extremely large, and there have recently been discoveries in Shanghai. A strict investigation should be carried out. Could the association submit a request to the government to stipulate that all rayon fabrics or interwoven fabrics produced by domestic silk weaving factories must be thoroughly investigated by the local silk weaving industry association to verify that smuggled rayon has not been used, and then issue a certificate before customs clearance and shipment? At the same time, the association should send personnel to each industry member in the city to conduct preliminary inspections to determine if smuggled rayon is being used, and issue certificates accordingly. Is this feasible? The meeting decided that the association should send letters to the Shanghai Silk and Rayon Industry Associations, urging them to pay close attention and convene a joint meeting of the three associations to discuss effective measures to inspect for smuggling.

Silk Mill Industry Association Cables Zhejiang Province to Release Detained Spring Cocoons 110

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the eighth executive meeting of the Silk Improvement Committee of the National Economic Commission decided that the price of raw silk should be 665 yuan, based on the average near and far term price in Yokohama and New York on the 15th, plus 10 yuan, combined with the cocoon recovery center price determined by reeling yield: improved seed cocoons, 280 catties dried and 450 catties reeled; 80 yuan for reeling labor; 26 yuan for cocoon collection expenses; the center price is set at 30 yuan per dan (a unit of weight) in the market. Local seed cocoons: 305 catties dried and 550 catties reeled; 100 yuan for reeling labor; 23 yuan for cocoon collection expenses; the center price is set at 21 yuan per dan in the market. The above center prices will be adjusted according to the silk price fluctuation based on reeling yield. Any significant increase or decrease in the silk price will be announced immediately and notified to the relevant authorities in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces for implementation. On May 15th, the near-term silk price in New York was $1.575 to $1.60 per pound, and the far-term silk price was $1.48 per pound. The current price in Japan was 705 Japanese yen per dan, and the far-term price was 689 Japanese yen per dan. The Zhejiang local seed cocoons started to be sold after May 20th, mostly stopping around May 30th. After the committee set the price on May 15th, the silk prices in New York and Yokohama gradually declined. On May 30th, the near-term price in New York was $1.44 and the far-term price was $1.39. The current price in Japan was 658 Japanese yen per dan, and the far-term price was 649 Japanese yen per dan. The silk price drop was almost a tenth of the value.

Zhejiang Province Proclamation

On May 26th, the Zhejiang Provincial Government issued a proclamation when the sale of local seed cocoons in Zhejiang Province was about to end: "Proclamation regarding the temporary measures for the control and management of cocoon collection during the spring period of the 25th year of the Zhejiang Provincial Silk Control Committee. The proclamation has been published and implemented by this government. During the cocoon collection period, if any cocoon trading houses or cocoon merchants engage in the following: 1. Opening a cocoon trading house without approval or registration; 2. Concealing or underreporting the amount of cocoons collected; 3. Collecting improved seed cocoons while only approved to collect local seed cocoons; 4. Reporting improved seed cocoons as local seed cocoons while approved to collect both local and improved seed cocoons; 5. Collecting both local and improved seed cocoons without approval to do so; 6. Failing to pay the fresh cocoon improvement fee and seed funds; 7. Smuggling cocoons out of the province without paying the fresh cocoon improvement fee and seed funds; 8. Failing to affix the fee payment certificate to the cocoon package when shipping dried cocoons, or affixing the fee payment certificate without an export permit; 9. Violating other regulations and disrupting the control and management policies, once verified, they will be punished with one or more of the following measures, depending on the severity of the circumstances: 1. Ordered to cease operations; 2. The cocoon trading house will be prohibited from re-establishing for three years; 3. The fees that should be paid will be doubled; 4. All dried cocoons will be confiscated, sold, and the proceeds will be used for rewards. Before the fresh cocoon improvement fee, seed funds, or fines are paid, a part or all of the collected spring cocoons will be detained. If necessary, they may be sold to offset the debt. In addition to instructing the county and municipal governments to instruct their subordinates, the cocoon collection offices in the region, to handle matters strictly and prevent fraud, this government is deeply concerned that our eyes and ears may not be sufficient. We hereby permit people in all areas to report to the cocoon collection offices in various districts, the county and municipal governments, and the public security bureaus. Those who are successful in reporting will be rewarded with half of the additional fees collected. The informant will receive 50%, the dried cocoon inspection office will receive 10%, the enforcement agency will receive 20%, and the military police handling the case will receive 20%. If the dried cocoon inspection office or the enforcement agency and the military police report the matter, the informant should also be given a reward, but they should not file false accusations based on personal grudges, lest they be punished instead. We hereby issue this proclamation to inform the public. Chairman Huang Zao Xiong; Silk Control Committee Chairman Zeng Yangfu."

Control Committee Approval

On May 27th, the Silk Mill Industry Association telegraphed Zhejiang Province: "To Chairman Huang of Zhejiang Province and the Silk Control Committee of Hangzhou: The procedures for shipping Zhejiang cocoons are delayed, Shanghai factories need materials, and workers are waiting to reel. We earnestly request that you instruct the cocoon collection districts to expedite the approval of shipping procedures. This is for the public convenience. Sincerely, the Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association." The Zhejiang Provincial Silk Control Committee replied: "Your telegram has been noted. If the cocoon merchants have paid all the fees they should pay, and the selling price of the local cocoons is above 21 yuan, they should be allowed to ship them quickly to benefit industry and commerce. In addition to instructing the district offices to comply, you are hereby informed. Committee Chairman Zeng Yangfu, May 29th, 25th year of the Republic of China."

Association Cables Again

The Silk Mill Industry Association telegraphed the Silk Improvement Committee of the National Economic Commission again the night before last: "According to reports from members, some factories purchased cocoons in Zhejiang Province at a slightly lower price and are being detained from shipping. Shanghai factories need materials, silk workers are waiting to reel, and the situation is critical. We plead to explain the difficulties. We respectfully note that your committee decided that the spring cocoon center price should be based on the size of the reeling yield and the silk price, and any significant increase or decrease should be announced. At that time, the price was set based on the New York and Yokohama silk market prices on May 15th. However, since the Zhejiang cocoon market opened on May 20th, the silk price has plummeted, with a difference of about 10% from before. Although this is not a significant difference, Shanghai factories have to consider costs. Moreover, the reeling yield varies from place to place. The meaning of the term 'center' is that it should not be too far from the standard. Therefore, the selling price may be slightly lower, but it is not intentional to violate the standard. We earnestly request your committee to examine the changes in the silk market and the difficulties of the silk merchants. Please forward this to the Zhejiang Provincial Government and the Silk Control Committee to waive the punishment, release the detained goods, and do a good deed for both parties. Sincerely, the Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association Committee." To the Silk Control Committee of Hangzhou: "According to reports from members, cocoons purchased in Zhejiang at a slightly lower price are being detained from shipping. Please explain the difficulties. We humbly believe that the National Economic Commission's Silk Improvement Committee stipulated the center price based on the silk price in the US and Japan and the reeling yield of fresh cocoons, and the cocoon price should fluctuate based on changes in the silk price and the reeling yield. However, since the cocoon market opened, the silk price has plummeted and the reeling yield varies from place to place. Silk merchants may have slightly lowered the selling price to protect their capital. This is not intentional to violate the standard. We humbly request you to be lenient, explain this to the provincial government, and instruct the districts to release the goods to relieve the difficulties. Sincerely, the Shanghai Silk Mill Industry Association."

Exchange Supervisor Discusses: Illegal Exchanges Will Not Be Realized; Exchange Law Stipulates That No Two Exchanges Can Exist in the Same Area 113

Xin Xin News Agency reports that there have been long-standing rumors about a certain foreigner planning to set up an illegal exchange in this port. A Xin Xin Du reporter specifically visited the Shanghai Exchange Supervisor to inquire about their opinion. They replied as follows: There have been long-standing rumors about a certain foreigner planning to set up an illegal exchange in this port. A Xin Xin Du reporter specifically visited the Shanghai Exchange Supervisor to inquire about their opinion. They replied as follows: I have heard about the incident of a certain foreigner planning to set up an exchange for a long time, but in reality, it may not be realized. Because the Chinese Exchange Law stipulates that "for exchanges dealing in securities or the same type of goods, only one exchange may be established in each area." Therefore, no two exchanges can exist within the same Shanghai area. In the past, the gold, securities, and cotton yarn sections of the commodity exchange were ordered to merge one after another because they conflicted with the Exchange Law. Those who understand the general principles must take into account international ethics, and legitimate businessmen will never have such illegal organizations. Moreover, among commodity trading, the one with the closest relationship with a certain country in the market is cotton yarn. However, the cotton yarn industry of a certain country joined the Chinese Cotton Cloth Market for trading last year, so there is no need to establish another exchange separately. Even if a part of unscrupulous merchants take risks, the concession authorities will never allow them to violate Chinese law and set up another market for business within the concession. Moreover, how could Chinese merchants who have a basic understanding of the overall situation join such an illegal exchange as brokers or traders to disrupt the inherent trading market in China and be traitors, earning the scorn of others? Moreover, since this exchange is not a legal organization, it is not protected by law. Those who are attracted to it will not only suffer losses but also be subject to the sanctions of national law. Based on these reasons, it is speculated that it may not become a reality.

The Chinese Farmers Bank; Banknotes Spread to Rural Areas; The Bank's Banknotes Are Allowed to Be Used in the Same Way as Legal Tender; Handling Rural Loans and Regulating Provincial Financial Affairs 115

The Chinese Farmers Bank was established to revitalize rural areas. After deliberation by the Legislative Yuan and the promulgation of regulations by the National Government, it was granted the right to issue banknotes. The bank was specially permitted to issue 100 million yuan of legal tender by order of the Ministry of Finance. It has successively handed over the required reserve fund to the Central Bank for safekeeping in accordance with the law, and followed the Ministry's order to use 50 million yuan to handle land and rural loans, focusing on the remote provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Sichuan, and Yunnan, and regulating rural finance. The bank's banknotes are used in the same way as the legal tender of the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. Therefore, various railways transport the bank's legal tender to regulate rural areas. It is understood that in order to make the people generally understand that the bank's banknotes are allowed to be used in the same way as the Central Bank, the Bank of Communications, and the Bank of China, it has specially submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to issue a circular to all provincial governments for public information, in order to increase the efficiency of use and achieve the goal of popularizing them in rural areas.
